<script>
var ref = document.getElementById("top-eq-2"),
    tgt = document.getElementById("top-eq-1"),
    img = tgt.getElementsByTagName("img")[0];

function formfirstblock()
{
    var elements = ref.getElementsByClassName("top-links-top-eq2");
    for (var i=0; i<elements.length; i++) {
        if ((elements[i].offsetTop + elements[i].offsetHeight) > (ref.offsetTop + ref.offsetHeight)) {
            elements[i].parentNode.removeChild(elements[i]);
            i--;
        }
    }

    var want = parseInt(tgt.offsetHeight-ref.offsetHeight),
        pp = tgt.getElementsByTagName("p")[0],
        ppLh = parseInt(getComputedStyle(pp).getPropertyValue("line-height")),
        ppL = parseInt(pp.offsetHeight/ppLh),
        diffL = Math.round(want/ppLh);

    if(diffL == ppL || diffL > ppL) {
        pp.style.display = "none";
        pp.remove();
    }

    if(diffL < ppL) {
        lines = parseInt(ppL-diffL);
        pp.style.height = parseInt(lines * ppLh)+"px";
        pp.style.WebkitLineClamp = lines;
        pp.style.display = 'block';
        pp.classList.add("trim-me");
    }

    var want2 = parseInt(ref.offsetHeight-tgt.offsetHeight),
        wrap = tgt.getElementsByClassName("content__info-wrap")[0];
    if(want2 < -20) {
        wrap.style.marginTop = "-20px";
    } else if(want2 <= 0) {
        wrap.style.marginTop = parseInt(want2)+"px";
    } else {
        wrap.style.paddingTop = parseInt(want2)+"px";
    }
}

if (img.complete) {
    formfirstblock();
} else if (img.addEventListener) {
    img.addEventListener('load', function() {
        formfirstblock();
    });
} else {
    img.attachEvent('onload', function() {
        formfirstblock();
    });
}

</script>

fishki.adblockCheckPassed = false;
fishki.is_adblock = true;

fishki.onAdblockEnabled = function(cb) {
    if (fishki.adblockCheckPassed) {
        if (fishki.is_adblock) {
            cb();
        }
    } else {
        $(window).on('adblock-enable', cb);
    }
};

fishki.onAdblockDisabled = function(cb) {
    if (fishki.adblockCheckPassed) {
        if (!fishki.is_adblock) {
           cb();
        }
    } else {
        $(window).on('adblock-disable', cb);
    }
};

fishki.onAdblockCheck = function (cbEnabled, cbDisabled) {
    fishki.onAdblockEnabled(cbEnabled);
    fishki.onAdblockDisabled(cbDisabled);
};

if (!fishki.adv) {
	fishki.adv = {}
}

fishki.sliders = (function() {

    function init_ticker($s) {
        var length = $s.find('.slide__item').length, mod = length % 5;
        if (mod)
            $('#the-ticker .slide__item:gt('+(length - mod-1)+')').remove();
        var parent_sizes = {};
        $(window).on('resize.the-ticker', function(){
            var $parent = null, resized = 0, $ticker = $('#the-ticker');
            $ticker.find('.slide__item.meta_image img, .slide__item.scale_image img').each(function(){
                if (!$parent)
                    $parent = $(this).parents('.slide__item');
                if (!parent_sizes)
                {
                    parent_sizes.width = $parent.width();
                    parent_sizes.height = $parent.height();
                }
                if (parent_sizes.width == $parent.width())
                    return;
                resized++;
                fishki.utils.resizeMeCenter(this, $parent.width(), $parent.height());
            });
            if (!resized)
                $(window).off('resize.the-ticker');
        });
        $(window).trigger('resize.the-ticker');
    }


	function slider_init()
	{
		var $slider = $('.cycle-slideshow:not(.inited)');
        $slider.each(function() {
            var $s = $(this);
            $s.addClass('inited');

            if (('showinlimbo' in window) && $s.find('.showlimbo_i').length)
                $s.find('.showlimbo_i').remove();
            if ($s.attr('id') === 'the-ticker')
                init_ticker($s);
            $s.on('cycle-prev cycle-next', function( event, opts ) {
                loadImages($s);
            });
            $s.cycle();
            $s.swipe();
        });

        $(function(){
            setTimeout(function() {
                $slider.each(function() {
                    loadImages($(this));
                });
            }, 1000)
        });

        $('img.lazy_load_image_past').each(function() {
			$(this).attr('src', $(this).data('src')).removeClass('lazy_load_image_past');
		});
	}

	function loadImages($slider)
	{
		if ($slider.find('img.lazy_load_image').length + $slider.find('a.lazy_load_image').length)
		{
			$slider.find('a.lazy_load_image').each(function(){
				var _this = this;
				$(_this).css('background-image', 'url(' + $(_this).data('src') + ')').ready(function() {
					$(_this).removeClass('lazy_load_image');
				});
			});

			$slider.find('img.lazy_load_image').each(function(){
				var _this = this;
				$(_this).attr('src', $(_this).data('src')).on('load', function() {
					$(_this).removeClass('lazy_load_image');
				});
			});
		}
	}

    function initthisslider(_this)
    {
        _this.removeClass('initthisslider');
        _this.find('.slider__arrow').unbind( "click" );
        var act = _this.find('.slider__arrow').data('action');
        var id = _this.find('.slider__arrow').data('id');
        _this.addClass('progress_slider_form');
        _this.find('.moderation').hide();
        _this.find('.progress_comment_img').show();
        $.ajax({
            type: 'post',
            data: 'action=' + act + '&id=' + id,
            url: '/getsimilar/',
            dataType: 'json',
            success: function(response) {
                if (response.hasOwnProperty('ok') && response.ok > 1) {
                    if (response.ok > 1) {
                        var hg = _this.height();
                        var wd = _this.width();
                        _this.parent().find('.toggles-wrap').remove();
                        _this.css('height', hg);
                        _this.css('overflow', 'hidden');
                        _this.find('.slide__item:last').after(response.html);
                        _this.attr('data-textid', 'textid_0');
                        _this.parent().find('.content__text:last').addClass('textid_0');
                        _this.parent().find('.content__text:last').after(response.html2);
                        _this.parent().find('.content__text:first').addClass('textid_0');
                        _this.parent().find('.content__text:first').after(response.html3);
                        _this.attr('data-cycle-fx', 'scrollHorz');
                        _this.attr('data-cycle-speed', 1000);
                        _this.attr('data-cycle-paused', true);
                        _this.attr('data-cycle-log', false);
                        _this.attr('data-cycle-slides', '.slide__item');
                        _this.attr('data-cycle-next', '>.slider__arrow--left');
                        _this.attr('data-cycle-prev', '>.slider__arrow--right');
                        var ln = (act=='next'?(_this.find('.slide__item').length-1):1);
                        _this.attr('data-starting-slide', ln);
                        _this.addClass('cycle-slideshow');
                        _this.parent().find('.content__text').addClass('hidden');
                        _this.parent().find('.textid_' + ln).removeClass('hidden');
                        _this.on( 'cycle-after', function(e, optionHash ) {
                            var sid = _this.find('.cycle-slide-active').data('textid');
                            _this.parent().find('.content__text').addClass('hidden');
                            _this.parent().find('.' + sid).removeClass('hidden');
                        });
                        var all = _this.find('.lazy_load_img img').length;
                        if (all > 0) {
                            _this.find('.lazy_load_img img').on('load', function() {
                                all--;
                                if (all == 0) {
                                    all--; // block
                                    _this.find('.lazy_load_img .post-img a>img').each(function() {
                                        var th = $(this);
                                        th.parent().parent().css('height', hg);
                                        var hg1 = th.height();
                                        var wd1 = th.width();
                                        if (wd1/hg1 > wd/hg) {
                                            th.css('height', hg);
                                            var wd2 = Math.floor(hg / hg1 * wd1) + 'px';
                                            var wd3 = '-' + Math.floor(hg / hg1 * wd1 / 2) + 'px';
                                            th.css('width', wd2);
                                            th.css('max-width', wd2);
                                            th.css('left', '50%');
                                            th.css('margin-left', wd3);
                                            th.css('position', 'absolute');
                                        } else {
                                            th.css('width', wd);
                                            var hd2 = Math.floor(wd / wd1 * hg1) + 'px';
                                            var hd3 = '-' + Math.floor(wd / wd1 * hg1 / 2) + 'px';
                                            th.css('height', hd2);
                                            th.css('max-height', hd2);
                                            th.css('top', '50%');
                                            th.css('margin-top', hd3);
                                            th.css('position', 'absolute');
                                        }
                                    });
                                    _this.find('.lazy_load_img').removeClass('lazy_load_img');
                                    _this.removeClass('progress_slider_form');
                                    _this.find('.progress_comment_img').hide();
                                    _this.cycle();
                                }
                            });
                        } else {
                            _this.cycle();
                        }
                    }
                } else {
                    _this.removeClass('progress_slider_form');
                    _this.find('.progress_comment_img').hide();
                }
            }
        });
    }

	function slider_sidebar()
    {
        $('.sidebar').not('.sidebar--hidden').find('.best_dem .sidebar__img img').one("load", function() {
            $(this).parents('a').addClass('black_back');
        })
    }
	return {
		init: slider_init,
		sidebar: slider_sidebar
	};
})();

	function author_arrow()
	{

		}
	}

	fishki.tpl = {
		author_arrow: author_arrow
	}
})();

    // ѕозици€ скролла при клике на элемент с анкором
    $(document).on('mouseover', '.header .nav__block__link', function(event)
    {
        var $this  = $(this);
        event.preventDefault();
        var target = $this.data('id');

        $this.parent('.nav__block__links').children('.nav__block__link').removeClass('active');
        $this.parent().parent().find('.nav__block__content').addClass('hidden');
        $this.addClass('active');
        $(target).removeClass('hidden');
    });

    $(document).on('click', '.header-settings__link_to', function(event)
    {
        var windWidth = window.innerWidth || document.documentElement.clientWidth || document.body.clientWidth;
        var $this     = $(this);
        var isSearch  = $this.hasClass('search');

        if ($this.hasClass('flag'))
            return;

        event.preventDefault();
        var val = $this.parent().hasClass('active');
        $('.header-settings__item').removeClass('active');

        if (!val) {
            $this.parent().addClass('active');

            if(isSearch && windWidth < 1024 && typeof fixDropMenu == 'function') {
                fixDropMenu($('.header-settings__item-search'));
            }
        }
            
    });
</script>

                    blockId: "R-A-561366-3",

            s = d.createElement("script");
            s.type = "text/javascript";
            s.src = "//an.yandex.ru/system/context.js";
            s.async = true;
            t.parentNode.insertBefore(s, t);
        })(this, this.document, "yandexContextAsyncCallbacks");
    }
</script>

<script data-enable="1">
	(function(){
		var updateSmi2Post = function(data) {
            if (data.news && data.news.length) {
                var i = Math.floor(Math.random() * data.news.length);
                $("#smi2-extended-1638537245").find(".post-link-1638537245").attr('href', data.news[i].url).end()
                    .find(".post-img-1638537245").attr('src', data.news[i].img).end()
                    .find(".post-title-1638537245").text(data.news[i].title).end()
                    .show();
            }
		};

		var session_key = "smi2-extended-smi", session_data = sessionStorage && sessionStorage.getItem(session_key);
		if (session_data)
			updateSmi2Post(JSON.parse(session_data));
		else
			$.ajax({
				url: "//news.smi2.ru/data/js/77803.js",
				dataType: 'json',
				async: true,
				success: function(data) {
					if (data.news && data.news[0] && data.news[0].img && data.news[0].title && data.news[0].url)
					{
						sessionStorage && sessionStorage.setItem(session_key, JSON.stringify(data));
						updateSmi2Post(data);
					} else if (data.photoreport) {
                        var g_data = {news: []};
                        var i = 0;
                        while (i<data.photoreport.length) {
                            if (data.photoreport[i] && data.photoreport[i]._url && data.photoreport[i]._name && data.photoreport[i].pic3) {
                                g_data.news.push({img: data.photoreport[i].pic3, title: data.photoreport[i].name, url: data.photoreport[i]._url});
                            }
                            i++;
                        }
                        if (g_data.news.length) {
                            sessionStorage && sessionStorage.setItem(session_key, JSON.stringify(g_data));
                            updateSmi2Post(g_data);
                        }
                    }
				},
				error:  function( xhr, textStatus ) {
					$("#smi2-extended-1638537245").hide().next('.content__separator').hide();
				}
			});

	})();
</script>
<script>
    $(window).on('adblock-enable', function(){
        $('a[href*="profile/543769"]').each(function(){
            var $el = $(this).parents('.drag_element');
            this.href="";
            if ($el.length)
            {
                if (!$el.hasClass('proceed'))
                {
                    $el.addClass('proceed');
                    setTimeout(function(){
                        $el.after($el.removeAttr('style').clone());
                        $el.hide();
                    }, 1000);
                }
            }
        });
    });
